data-testid="container" class="fixed-width gutters body03   " data-cas-id="c8nxKEflq"><h4 data-com-id="Text" class="font-demi text-size-inherit font-text-weight-inherit" data-sb-field-path=".text">TurboTax Online: Important Details about Filing Form 1040 Returns with Limited Credits</h4><p data-com-id="Text" class="pb-20 text-size-inherit font-text-weight-inherit" data-cas-id="c2ZT5yrIn" data-sb-field-path=".text">A Form 1040 return with limited credits is one that's filed using IRS Form 1040 only (with the exception of the specific covered situations described below). Roughly 37% of taxpayers are eligible.<br><br>If you have a Form 1040 return and are claiming limited credits only, you can file for free yourself with TurboTax Free Edition, or you can file with TurboTax Live Assisted Basic or TurboTax Full Service at the listed price.<br></p><div data-com-id="RichText" class="mb-16 text-size-inherit" data-cas-id="c87kAlqrS" data-sb-field-path=".htmlContent"><p class="font-demi body03">Situations covered (assuming no added tax complexity):</p>
<ul class="body03">
<li>W-2 income</li>
<li>Interest or dividends (1099-INT/1099-DIV) that don’t require filing a Schedule B</li>
<li>IRS standard deduction</li>
<li>Earned Income Tax Credit (EITC)</li>
<li>Child Tax Credit (CTC)</li>
<li>Student loan interest deduction</li>
</ul>
<p class="font-demi body03">Situations not covered:</p>
<ul class="body03">
<li>Itemized deductions claimed on Schedule A</li>
<li>Unemployment income reported on a 1099-G</li>
<li>Business or 1099-NEC income</li>
<li>Stock sales (including crypto investments)</li>
<li>Rental property income</li>
<li>Credits, deductions and income reported on other forms or schedules </li>
</ul></div><div data-com-id="Expandable" data-testid="expandable-container" class="

<h3 class="body02 font-demi pt-12">TURBOTAX ONLINE/MOBILE PRICING</h3>
<ul>

Roughly 37% of taxpayers qualify. Offer may change or end at any time without notice. <br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">TurboTax Live Assisted Basic Offer:</span> Offer only available with TurboTax Live Assisted Basic and for those filing Form 1040 and limited credits only. Roughly 37% of taxpayers qualify. Must file between November 29, 2023 and March 31, 2024 to be eligible for the offer. Includes state(s) and one (1) federal tax filing. Intuit reserves the right to modify or terminate this TurboTax Live Assisted Basic Offer at any time for any reason in its sole and absolute discretion. If you add services, your service fees will be adjusted accordingly. If you file after 11:59pm EST, March 31, 2024, you will be charged the then-current list price for TurboTax Live Assisted Basic and state tax filing is an additional fee. <a href="https://turbotax.intuit.com/personal-taxes/online/live/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">See current prices here.</a><br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Full Service $100 Back Offer:</span> Credit applies only to federal filing fees for TurboTax Full Service and not returns filed using other TurboTax products or returns filed by Intuit TurboTax Verified Pros. Excludes TurboTax Live Full Service Business <span style="font-weight: 400;">and TurboTax Canada products</span>. Credit does not apply to state tax filing fees or other additional services. If federal filing fees are less than $100, the remaining credit will be provided via electronic gift card. Intuit reserves the right to modify or terminate this offer at any time for any reason in its sole discretion. <span style="font-weight: 400;">Must file by April 15, 2024 11:59 PM ET.</span><br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">TurboTax Full Service - Forms-Based Pricing:</span> “Starting at” pricing represents the base price for one federal return (includes one W-2 and one Form 1040). Final price may vary based on your actual tax situation and forms used or included with your return. Price estimates are provided prior to a tax expert starting work on your taxes. Estimates are based on initial information you provide about your tax situation, including forms you upload to assist your expert in preparing your tax return and forms or schedules we think you’ll need to file based on what you tell us about your tax situation. Final price is determined at the time of print or electronic filing and may vary based on your actual tax situation, forms used to prepare your return, and forms or schedules included in your individual return. Prices are subject to change without notice and may impact your final price. If you decide to leave Full Service and work with an independent Intuit TurboTax Verified Pro, your Pro will provide information about their individual pricing and a separate estimate when you connect with them.<br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Pays for itself (TurboTax Premium, formerly Self-Employed): </span>Estimates based on deductible business expenses calculated at the self-employment tax income rate (15.3%) for tax year 2022. Actual results will vary based on your tax situation.</li>
</ul>

Online competitor data is extrapolated from press releases and SEC filings. “Online” is defined as an individual income tax DIY return (non-preparer signed) that was prepared online & either e-filed or printed, not including returns prepared through desktop software or FFA prepared returns, 2022.<br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">CompleteCheck:</span> Covered under the TurboTax accurate calculations and maximum refund <a href="https://turbotax.intuit.com/corp/guarantees/" target="_blank" rel="noopener" data-toggle="modal">guarantees</a>. Limitations apply. See <a href="https://turbotax.intuit.com/corp/license/online/" target="_blank" rel="noreferrer noopener">Terms of Service</a><a href="https://turbotax.intuit.com/corp/license/online" target="_blank" rel="noopener"> </a>for details.</li>
</ul>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-demi">TurboTax Premium Pricing Comparison:</span> Cost savings based on a comparison of TurboTax product prices to average prices set forth in the 2020-2021 NSA Fees-Acct-Tax Practices Survey Report.<br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">1099-K Snap and Autofill:</span> Available in mobile app and mobile web only.<br><br></li>

Available in mobile app only. Feature available within Schedule C tax form for TurboTax filers with 1099-NEC income.<br><br></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Year-Round Tax Estimator:</span> Available in TurboTax Premium (formerly Self-Employed) and TurboTax Live Assisted Premium (formerly Self-Employed). This product feature is only available after you finish and file in a self-employed TurboTax product.<br><br></li>

<li><span class="font-demi">TurboTax Online Business Products:</span> For TurboTax Live Assisted Business and TurboTax Full Service Business, we currently don’t support the following tax situations: C-Corps (Form 1120-C), Trust/Estates (Form 1041), Multiple state filings, Tax Exempt Entities/Non-Profits, Entities electing to be treated as a C-Corp, Schedule C Sole proprietorship, Payroll, Sales tax, Quarterly filings, and Foreign Income. <span class="font-demi">TurboTax Live Assisted Business is currently available only in AK, AZ, CA, CO, FL, GA, IL, KS, MA, MD, ME, MI, MO NC, NJ, NV, NY, OH, PA, SD, TN, TX, UT, VA, WA, WV, and WY.</span> <br><br></li>

<p>TurboTax Desktop Individual Returns:</p>
<ul>
<li><span class="font-demi">100% Accurate Calculations Guarantee – Individual Returns: </span>If you pay an IRS or state penalty or interest because of a TurboTax calculation error, we’ll pay you the penalty and interest. Excludes payment plans. This guarantee is good for the lifetime of your personal, individual tax return, which Intuit defines as seven years from the date you filed it with TurboTax Desktop. Excludes TurboTax Desktop Business returns. Additional terms and limitations apply. See <a class="link-demi-underline" href="/corp/license/desktop.jsp">License Agreement</a> for details.<br /><br /></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Maximum Refund Guarantee / Maximum Tax Savings Guarantee - or Your Money Back – Individual Returns:</span> If you get a larger refund or smaller tax due from another tax preparation method by filing an amended return, we'll refund the applicable TurboTax federal and/or state software license purchase price you paid. This guarantee is good for the lifetime of your personal, individual tax return, which Intuit defines as seven years from the date you filed it with TurboTax Desktop. Excludes TurboTax Desktop Business returns. Additional terms and limitations apply. See <a class="link-demi-underline" href="/corp/license/desktop.jsp">License Agreement</a> for details.<br /><br /></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Audit Support Guarantee – Individual Returns: </span>If you receive an audit letter from the IRS or State Department of Revenue based on your 2023 TurboTax individual tax return, we will provide one-on-one question-and-answer support with a tax professional, if requested through our <a rel="noreferrer noopener" href="https://ttlc.intuit.com/turbotax-support/en-us/help-article/intuit-account-billing/turbotax-audit-support-guarantee/L06x5FWbz_US_en_US" target="_blank">Audit Support Center</a>, for audited individual returns filed with TurboTax Desktop for the current 2023 tax year and, for individual, non-business returns, for the past two tax years (2021, 2022). Audit support is informational only. We will not represent you before the IRS or state tax authority or provide legal advice. If we are not able to connect you to one of our tax professionals, we will refund the applicable TurboTax federal and/or state license purchase price you paid. This guarantee is good for the lifetime of your personal, individual tax return, which Intuit defines as seven years from the date you filed it with TurboTax Desktop. Excludes TurboTax Desktop Business returns. Additional terms and limitations apply. See <a class="link-demi-underline" href="/corp/license/desktop.jsp">License Agreement</a> for details.<br /><br /></li>
<li><span class="font-demi">Satisfaction Guarantee/ 60-Day Money Back Guarantee:</span> If you're not completely satisfied with TurboTax Desktop, go to refundrequest.intuit.com within 60 days of purchase and follow the process listed to submit a refund request. You must return this product using your license code or order number and dated receipt.</li>

data-testid="gridItem-element" class=" sm:flex body03 GridItem-sm:col-span-5-0e11454  GridItem-order-24bcdbf undefined"><div data-com-id="Container" data-testid="container" class="inline-block   "><a class="Link-font-demi-link-c76ff4c pr-12 mr-12 border-r border-pepper100" data-com-id="Link" href="https://security.intuit.com/index.php/intuit-cookie-policy/"><span data-com-id="Text" class=" data-com-id="Image" newKey="New Value" id="privacy-modal-link-logo"><img class="" src="https://digitalasset.intuit.com/content/dam/intuit/cg/en_us/images/icons/privacy-options.svg" alt="Privacy setting" style="height:19px" data-testid="xs-pic-src" loading="lazy"/></picture></span></div><div data-com-id="GridItem" data-testid="gridItem-element" class="  GridItem-sm:col-span-4-e892d71  GridItem-order-24bcdbf undefined"><div data-com-id="Container" data-testid="container" class="flex justify-start md:justify-end pt-20 pb-20   "><div data-com-id="Codeblock"><div><a href="//privacy.trustarc.com/privacy-seal/validation?rid=7fc012b5-d53b-42d8-b980-c4f9091a97e1" target="_blank"><img style="border: none" src="//hostedseal.trustarc.com/privacy-seal/seal?rid=7fc012b5-d53b-42d8-b980-c4f9091a97e1" alt="TRUSTe" width="104" height="“33”/"></a></div></div><picture data-com-id="Image"><img class="mr-20 ml-20" src="https://digitalasset.intuit.com/content/dam/intuit/cg/en_us/turbotax/ttcom/seals/irs-efile.svg" alt="eFile" style="height:20px" data-testid="xs-pic-src" loading="lazy"/></picture><a class="Link-font-demi-link-c76ff4c " data-com-id="Link" href="http://clevelsecurity.com/certified/intuit/Intuit_turbotax.html"><picture data-com-id="Image"><img class="" src="https://digitalasset.intuit.com/content/dam/intuit/cg/en_us/turbotax/ttcom/seals/clevel.svg" alt="clevel" style="height:20px" data-testid="xs-pic-src" loading="lazy"/></picture></a></div></div></div><div data-com-id="Codeblock" data-cas-id="c2TluBrU1"><script type="application/javascript">
(function() {
  const getCookie = (name) => {
    for (const c of document.cookie.split('; ')) {
      const key = `${name}=`;
      if (!c.startsWith(key)) continue;
      return c.substr(key.length);
    }
  };

  const geo = getCookie("AKES_GEO_OVERRIDE") || getCookie("AKES_GEO");
  const linkText = document.querySelector("#privacy-modal-link-text");
  const linkLogo = document.querySelector("#privacy-modal-link-logo");

  if (geo !== "US~CA") {
    if (linkText) linkText.innerText = "Manage Cookies";
    if (linkLogo) linkLogo.style.visibility = "hidden";
